1b1(phal chen): /sangs rgyas pal po che las/sdong pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste/
1b2(phal chen): bam po brgya gcig go//de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nir bzangs mtshan mo'i lha mo
1b3(phal chen): sems can kun tu skyong ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par
1b4(phal chen): thar pa'i 'jig rten thams cad mngon du gyur pas 'gro ba rnam par 'dul ba de la
2a1(phal chen): par bya ba dang /shin tu rgyas par bya ba dang /yongs su khyab par bya ba dang /rag tus rnyed par bya
2a2(phal chen): dang /dbang du bya ba dang /spong bar thu ba dang /yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba byed cing /mtshan mo'i nam
2a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho rab tu ni ba dang ldan pa gang na pa der phyin te/mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu na pa dang ldan pa'i rkang pa ga
2a4(phal chen): la skye bos phyag 'tshal /mam ze'i wa so sa mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa par
2b1(phal chen): stong du mar g.yas phyogs su bskor ba byas nas/mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i mdun du 'dug ste/thal
2b2(phal chen): mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smras so//'phags ma lha mo bdag ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du yang dag par zhug pa
2b3(phal chen): ste/bdag ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rten gyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la slob cing byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa
2b4(phal chen): la zhugs te/byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la nan tan du bgyi ba dang /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la rab tu gnas
2b5(phal chen): pas/thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'byung bar 'tshal na/'phags ma lha mo ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems
2b6(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bgyi ba dang /ji ltar nan tan du bgyi ba bdag la bshad du gsol/de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo sla
3a1(phal chen): rgya mtsho rab tu zhi bu dang ldan pas/tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smraso//rigs kyi
3a2(phal chen): bu de ltar khyod dge ba'i bo shes gnyen gyi rten gyis/byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongasasu tshol ba legaso leg so//rigs
3a3(phal chen): kyi bu kho mo ni byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yongs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa
3a4(phal chen): thob pa'o//ni ra bzangs kyis smras pa/'phags ma khyod ni phrin las ci mdzad/yul gang dang ldan/sbyor ba gang dang ldan /
3a5(phal chen): ji la rnam par spyod/byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas/sems kyi skad cig rnam
3a6(phal chen): par brgyan pa de'i yul ni ji lta bu zhig mchis/des smras pa/rigs kyi bu kho mo ni sems dang bsam pa rgya mtsho yongasu dag pa'i
3b1(phal chen): mnyam pa nyid du zhugs pa ste/'jig rten gyi rdul dri ma thams cad rnam par bsal bsu mi byed pas brgyan pa'i bsam pa la zhugs pa'o//
3b2(phal chen): brnams pa lis mi ldog/mi ldog pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o//rin po che'i ri bo ltor yon tan gyis brgyan pa'i sems mi sgul bya dang ldan
3b3(phal chen): pa'o//mi gnas mi rten pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o//'gro ba thams cad yongasasu skyabs pa la mngon par phyogs pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o//sangs
3b4(phal chen): rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad mthong bas mi ngoms pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o//byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi stobs kyis bsam pa rnam par dag pa'i
3b5(phal chen): sems dang ldan pa'o//dran pa'i rgya mtsho ye shes kyi snang ba chen pos brgyan pa la yang dag par gnas pa'i sems dang ldan pa'o//sems can thams
3b6(phal chen): cad mya ngan gyi dgon pa las yang dag par bzla ba la zhugs pa'o//sems can thams cad sdug bsngal dang /yid mi bde ba las rnam par bzlog
3b7(phal chen): pa la mngon par brtson pa'o//sems can thams cad kyi yid du mi 'ong ba'i gzugs dang /sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg yongasasu rgyu ba rnam par bzlog pa la
4a1(phal chen): /zhugs pa'o//sems can thams cad kyi sdug pa dang mi sdug pa dang bral zhing phrad pa'i sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar bya ba la zhugs pa'o//
4a2(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi yul gyi rkyen las byung bas mgo rmongs pa'i sdug bsngal rnam par bzlog pa la rab tu brten pa'o//log par ltung ba'i sems can thams
4a3(phal chen): cad kyi rten du gyur pa'o//sems can thams cad 'khor ba'i gnas kyi sdug bsngal las 'byung ba yang dag par ston pa la mngon par brtson pa'o//sems can
4a4(phal chen): ngoms cad kyi rga shi dang mya ngan drang smre sngags 'don pa dang /sdug bsngal ba dang //yid mi bde ba dang 'khrug pa rnam par bzlog pa la zhugs pa'o//sems
4a5(phal chen): can thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i bde ba bla na med pa yongasu bsgrub par zhugs pa ste/grong dang grong khyer dang /ljongs dang /yul dang khams dang /rgyal
4a6(phal chen): blo'i gnas na 'khrod pa'i sems can thams cad bdi bar rim gror bya bas/nyams dga' bar 'gyur zhing de dag la chos dang mthun par bsrung ba dang /bsgrub po dang /
4a7(phal chen): rim gro bya ba yang legs par byed/de dag rim pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongasu srin par byed//'di lta ste khang khyim dang /gzhal ma khang ni gnos pa'i
4b1(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi mngon par chags pa med pa yongs su skyed//yid mi bde ba de dang de dag kyang rnam par sel to//mngon par zhen pa thams cad rgyun bcud pa dang /chos
4b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi rang bzhin yongasu shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//pha ma dang phu nu dang /sring mo dang gnyen pa shes dang 'grogs pa'i sems can yun ring po nas ba shes
4b3(phal chen): shing mdza' bar gyur pa dag las sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang phrad par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//bu rmad dang 'grogs pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i
4b4(phal chen): sred pa thams cad rab tu spang ba dang /sems can thams cad la mnyam pa nyid kyi semasu bya ba dang /snying rje chen po rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//tshong 'dus kyi//
4b5(phal chen): dbus na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la 'phags pa'i dge 'dun dang /de bzhin gshegs pa mthong bar bya ba la yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//
4b6(phal chen): longs spyod kyi dregs pas myos pa'i sems can rnams la bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//glu dang gar dang rol mo la mngon par dga'
4b7(phal chen): ba'i sems can rnams la chos kyi dga' ba la mos par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//yul gyi dga' ba la chags pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la
5a1(phal chen): yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//khro bas yongs su non pa'i sems can rnams la bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu dgod par bya ba'i phyir chos
5a2(phal chen): ston to//sems can le lo can rnams la brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston/sems rnam par myos pa'i sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs
5a3(phal chen): pa'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//lta ba'i rnam pa thibs por srubs pa'i sems can ma rig pa'i mun nag 'thom pa rnams la lta ba'i rnam pa
5a4(phal chen): thibs po dang /ma rig pa'i mun pa rnam par bsal ba'i phyir chos ston to//shes rab 'chal ba can gyi sems can rnams la/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir
5a5(phal chen): chos ston to//khams gsum pa la mngon par zhon pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba las 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//dma' ba la mos pa'i sems can rnams la/de bzhin
5a6(phal chen): gshegs pa'i byang chub tu smon lam yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//bdag la phan par brtson pa'i sems can rnams la sems can thams cad la phan par bya ba'i smon
5a7(phal chen): lam yongasu rdzogs par 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//bsam pa nyam chung ba'i sems can+da rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag par bya
5b1(phal chen): ba'i phyir chos ston to//ma rig pa'i mun pas sems blong ba'i sems can rnams la/byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//
5b2(phal chen): gzugs mi sdug pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la/de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzugs kyi sku rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//lus kyi dbyings mi mdzes pa dang ldan pa'i
5b3(phal chen): sems can rnams la chos kyi sku bla na med pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//kha dog mi sdug pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la/de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mdog gser
5b4(phal chen): gyi kha dog lta bu dang /shin tu 'jam zhing ka tsa li 'da' ltar reg na bde ba'i lus rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//sdug bsngal ba'i sems can rnams la/de bzhin
5b5(phal chen): gshegs pa'i bde ba dam pa rab tu thob pa'i phyir chos ston to//bde ba'i sems can rnams la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bde ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//nad pa na ba'i
5b6(phal chen): sems can rnams la/byang chub sems dpa'i lus gzugs brnyan lta bu yongasu grub par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//dga' ba sna tshogs lo brtson pa'i sems can rnams la/byang
5b7(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i dga' ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston te//phongs pa'i sems can rnams la/byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi gter dang mdzod rab tu thob par bya ba'i
6a1(phal chen): phyir chos ston to//bza' shing gi sha na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la/sangs rgyas kyi chos yongasu btsal ba mngon par brtson pa'i rgyu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston//
6a2(phal chen): to//lam du zhugs pa'i sems can rnams la/thams cad mkhyen pa'i lam du 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//grong na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la/khams gsum
6a3(phal chen): bapa thams cad las 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//yul gyi mdab na gnas pa'i sems can rnams la/nyan thos dang rang byang chub kyi lam las yang dag par 'da' bar bya ba
6a4(phal chen): dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la rab tu dgod par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//grong rdal na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la/chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang gnas par 'gyur ba'i
6a5(phal chen): phyir chos ston to//phyogs mtshams na 'khod pa'i sems can rnams la/dus gsum mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//phyogs na gnas pa'i sems
6a6(phal chen): can rnams la/chos thams cad kyi ye shes mngon par shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//'dod chags la gcig tu dga' ba'i sems can rnams la mi sdug pa'i sgos 'khor ba'i
6a7(phal chen): sred pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos ston to//zhe sdang la spyod pa'o sems can rnams la byams pa chen po'i tshul rgya mtsho la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//gti mug la spyod
6b1(phal chen): pa'i sems can rnams la chos thams cad kyi sgo rgya mtsho rab tu 'byed pa'i ye shes mngon par shes par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//cha mnyam pa la spyod pa'i sems can rnams la/thog
6b2(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi smon lam gyi tshul rgya mtshos khyad par du 'gro bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//'khor ba'i yul gyi dga' bo'i bsam pa can gyi sems can rnams la/'khor ba'i yul
6b3(phal chen): dga' ba rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir chos ston to//'khor ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad kyis gtses pa'i sems can rnams la 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal thams cad kyis nye bar nyon mongs
6b4(phal chen): pab med par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la/mi skye ba'i gnas yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir chos ston to//phung po la gnas pa'i
6b5(phal chen): bsam pa can gyi sems can rnams la/gzhi med pa'i chos kyi spyod yul la rnam par spyod par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//bsam pa zhum pa'i sems can rnams la lam gyi rgyan gyi
6b6(phal chen): khyad par yang dag par bstan par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//mtho ba'i nga rgyal can gyi sems can rnams la chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi bzod pa yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir chos
6b7(phal chen): ston to//g.yo sgyu'i yul gyi bsam pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams la/byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa yongasu dag par bya ba'i phyir chos ston to//de ltar rigs kyi bu kho mo na
7a1(phal chen): sems can thams cad chos kyi sbyin pas yongasu bsdus shing ngan song gi lam gyi rgyud sdug bsngal ba thams cad nas/rnam par bzlog pa dang lha dang mi'i
7a2(phal chen): phun sum tshogs pa dang /bde ba yongasu bstan pa dang /khams gsum pa las gyen du bskyod pa dang /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la rab tu dgod pa dang /thabs sna tshogs kyis
7a3(phal chen): yongasu smin par byed byed pas dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho snang ba rab tu thob pas dga'o zhing spro la yid bde bar gyur pa'o//gzhan yang rigs kyi bu kho mo ni phyogs dang /
7a4(phal chen): phyogs mtshams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho la rnam par lta zhing smon lam rgya mtsho la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' lus sna tshogs rnam par dag
7a5(phal chen): pa 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sna tshogs kyi rgyan dang ldan pa 'od gzer dang 'od kyi dkyil 'khor kha dog mtha' yas pa rab tu 'gyed pa/thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshul rgya mtsho sna chog
7a6(phal chen): la zhugs pa'i ye shes snyam pa can ting 'dzin rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyi yul dang ldan pa/dbyangs kyi yan lag dang /skad rgya mtsho
7a7(phal chen): tshogs kyi dbyangs dang ldan pa/rgyan sna tshogs kyis rnam par grubs pa'i lus can/de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs la zhugs pa zhing rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa sna
7b1(phal chen): tshog su zhugs pa'i lus dang ldan pa/sangs rgyas rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa rgya mtsho sna tshogs la zhugs pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par ngar
7b2(phal chen): pa dang /ye shes kyi yul sna tshogs kyis snang bar gyur pa/ye shes rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi snang ba rab tu thob pa/ting 'dzin rgya mtsho sna tshogs kyi tshul la rnam par spyod pa chos sna tshogs
7b3(phal chen): kyis rnam par thar pa'i gzha med khang rnam par rtse ba'i yul dang ldan pa/thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo sna tshogs la mngon du gnas pa chos kyi dbyings sna tshogs kyi na mkha'i rgyan
7b4(phal chen): dang ldan pa/rgyan sna tshogs kyi sprin gyis na mkha' rgyas par 'gengs pa/'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho sna tshogs la rnam par lta ba/'jig rten gyi khams sna tshogs nas 'dus pa/
7b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing sna tshogs 'byam klas par rjes su 'dong ba phyogs rgya mtsho sna tshogs nas yongs 'dus pa/de bzhin gshegs pa tha dad pas bkye ba/de bzhin gshegs pa tha dad
7b6(phal chen): pa'i zhabs kyi drung nas lhags po/byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs sna tshogs kyi 'khor dang ldan pa/rgyan sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi char rab tu 'debs pa/de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul
7b7(phal chen): sna tshogs la zhugs pa/de bzhin gau shig pa'i chos rgya mtsho sna tshogs la rnam par spyod pa ye shes sna tshogs rgya mtsho la zhugs pa/brgyan gyi snying po sna tshogs can gyi stan la
8a1(phal chen): 'khod pa rnams kyi dga' bo sna tshogs kyi shugs rgya mtsho yongasu skyed de/de dag dga' ba sna tshogs kyi shugs rgya mtsho yongasu skyes nas/de bzhin gshegs
8a2(phal chen): pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtshor 'dong ste/de dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs tshod med pa rjesu sems pas kyang /dga' ba'i shugs chen po rgya mtsho yong su 'byung bar 'gyuraro///
8a3(phal chen): rigs kyi bu gzhan yang /kho mo ni bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi gzugs kyi sku yongasu dag pa mtshan gyis rab tu brgyan pa bsam gyis mi khyad pa/mthong nas dga' ba chen po
8a4(phal chen): dang /mos pa shing nyams bde ba rab tu 'thob ste/sems kyi skad cig re re la'ang 'od kyi dkyil 'khor chos kyi dbyings ltar yangs pa kha dog rgya mtsho mthar dang dbung med par snang ba
8a5(phal chen): la lta zhing sems kyi skad cig re re la dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho rab tu 'tho'o//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku'i ba spu'i sgo re re nas kyang
8a6(phal chen): 'od gzer chen po sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' dang dpung med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste/'od gzer re re zhing yang /'od gzer rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' yas pa'i rdul
8a7(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'khor dang ldan pas/chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa dang /sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar mdzad pa mthong zhing sems kyi
8b1(phal chen): s+yAd cagA re re la/dga' 'a chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho ba tu 'thob pa//rigs rgyu bu gzhan yang /bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi bu dang /sru phrag pa gnyis kyi ldan las/sems
8b2(phal chen): kyi skud cig re ra la rin po chu thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba'i ri'i sbyin/sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba rnyed 'byung zhing chos kyi dbyings rgya mchi thams cad rgya par 'gengs pa
8b3(phal chen): ma na myu ga' chen po thugs mtsho byin rgyal su rji tu 'amag//gas kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgra rgyun sko ra nas sems kyi smra
8b4(phal chen): kha dag rdzogam pa dang /'od gzer sna tshogs can gyi sbyin/sangs sa m+b+ha na rnams rlung gyi rdus shi tsa bye ba snyid 'byung zhing /sangs na mi ldan bams cad rgyam par 'gasapa
8b5(phal chen): mthong nas/dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/sems
8b6(phal chen): skad cig re re la mtshan re re nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs mtshan gyis rab tu brgyan pa'i sbyin/sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste/'jig rten gyi
8b7(phal chen): /khams rgya mtsha thams cad rgyam par 'gengs pa mthong nas/dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu langs parab tu 'thob bo//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam pa
9a1(phal chen): snang mdzad kyi sku'i dpe byad bzang po re re las/sems kyi skad cig re rI la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku dpe byang bdang po brgyad nus shin tu 'ab
9a2(phal chen): ba'i sprin/sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ste/sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rgyas par 'gengs shing /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi
9a3(phal chen): 'khor lo'i dbyangasu sgrog pa'i 'brug sgra 'byin pa mthong nas/dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam
9a4(phal chen): bar snang mdzad kyi sku le rnam par bltas na/sems kyi skad cig re ra la ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas/sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa'i sku dang po byang chub tu thugs bskyed pa dang bcas
9a5(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa'i lam rnam par dag pa'i rgyan dang bcas/byang chub sems dpa'i sa yongasasu gnon pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang /bcas pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul
9a6(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung ba mthong nas/dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi
9a7(phal chen): sku las sems kyi skad cig re re la lha'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin lha'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung
9b1(phal chen): zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/lha'i dbang po'i lus yongasu bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon tu gnas shing chos ston pa mthong nas dga'
9b2(phal chen): ba chen po'i shug rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob bo//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku las sems kyi skad cig re re la klu'i dbang po'i lus kyi
9b3(phal chen): sprin/klu'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/klu'i dbang po'i

9b6(phal chen): gyi dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/gnod sbyin gyi lus

10a2(phal chen): sprin dri za'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyad byung zhing /chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/dri za

10a7(phal chen): 'thob bo//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo re ro nas na mkha' lding gi dbang po'i lus
10b1(phal chen): kyi sprin na mkha' lding gi dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/
10b2(phal chen): namakha' lding gi dbang po'i lus yongasu bstan pas 'dul ba'i sems can rnams la mngon du gnas shing chos ston pa mthong nas/dga' ba chen po'i shags rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pa
10b3(phal chen): rab tu 'thog//gzhan yang rigs kyi bu bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rnam par bltas na/sems kyi skad cig re re la ba spu'i sgo re re nas mi 'am ci'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin
10b4(phal chen): mi 'am ci'i dbang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang bcas pa/sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung zhing /chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/mi 'am

11b1(phal chen): re la/thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i dga' ba chen po'i shugs rgya mtsho chos kyi dbyings ltar rgya che zhing shin tu yangs pa rab tu 'thob ste/sngon thob par gyur pa 'thob par 'gyur/
11b2(phal chen): nga ma yin//sngon khong du chud pa khong du chud par 'gyur ba ma yino//sngon zhugs pa la 'jug par 'gyur ba ma yin//sngon khyab par gyur pa khyab par 'gyur ba ma yin//sngon mthong ba
11b3(phal chen): mthong bar 'gyur ba ma yin no//sngon thos pa thos par 'gyur ba ma yin no//de ci'i phyir zhe na/chos kyi rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid yongasu shes pa ltar na/chos thams cad mtshan nyid
11b4(phal chen): gcig pa'ang ci rab ma yin te/dus gsum gyi tshul 'jug pa'i sgor zhugs na/chos thams cad kyang mtha' dang dpung med par bstan du yod pa ste/'di ni rigs kyi bu byang chub sems
11b5(phal chen): dpa'i rnam par thar pa'i tshul dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa'i tshul rgya mtsho'i snang ba ste/rigs kyi bu rnam par thar pa 'di ni/chos kyi

12a1(phal chen): rgyas par 'gengs pas gting med pa'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni/dmigs pa gcig tu rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongasu 'du bar byed pas sgo thams
12a2(phal chen): cad dang ldan pa'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni/chos thams cad kyi lus dang mi gnyis par spyod pas don yod pa'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni sgyu ma lta bur yongasu spyod pas ma skyes
12a3(phal chen): ba'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni/thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi smon lam gyi gzugs brnyan du byung bas gzugs brnyan lta bu'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni/byang chub sems dpa'i
12a4(phal chen): spyod pas shin tu sprul pa'i phyir sprul pa lta bu'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi rten du gyur pas sa tshon po lta bu'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni 'gro ba thams
12a5(phal chen): tsid snying rje chen pos mngon par brlan par byed pas tshu'i phung po lta bu'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni sems can thams cad kyi sred pa'i rlon yongasu skems pas ma'i phung po lta

13a1(phal chen): pa 'di ni/mi shigs pa'i chos can yin pas rdo rje lta bu'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni/rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' dang dpung med pa rgya mtsho mngon par sgrub pas nor/

13a3(phal chen): med pas rin po che'i rgyal po dri ma med pa'i snying po lta bu'o//rnam par thar pa 'di ni/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo mnyam pa nyid du sgrog pas nor bu rin po che dga' ba'i

13b3(phal chen): chub sems dpa' tshul khrims de bzhin gshegs pa'i ston rgya mtsho la 'jug pa'i nan tan la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so//byang chub sems dpa'i bzod pa chos thams cad
13b4(phal chen): rang bzhin nges par rdzogs par bya ba la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so//byang chub sems dpa'i brtson 'grus thams cad mkhyen po nyid du yang dag par brtsams pa las phyir mi ldog

13b7(phal chen): smyon par bya ba dang /gdul ba la zhugs pa ni/chen gyi chos so//byang chub sems da pa'i sprin lam phyim motsho'i mu thug pa'i bskal par sangs rgyas kyinang thams cad du byang
14a1(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad pa'i phyir zhing rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so//byang chub sems dpa'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad//
14a2(phal chen): du skad cig re re la mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar yongasu bstan pa rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir/chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsha thams cad la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i chos so//
14a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes dus gsum gyi chos thams cad la sgrib pa med pa'i ye shes thob par bya ba'i phyir/de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs la zhugs pa ni rgya chen po'i
14a4(phal chen): chos so//rigs kyi bu bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgya chen po'i chos tshogs chen po dang ldan pa rnams te/de dag la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam
14a5(phal chen): kyis rnam par thar pa de lta bu phun sum tshogs par 'gyur//rnam par dag par 'gyur ro//yongasu 'byung bar 'gyuraro//yang dag par 'brel bar 'gyuraro//kun nas 'byung

14b1(phal chen): rigs kyi bu 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi me tog gi snying po'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa 'di'i shar phyogs log su 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho stong phrag bcu 'das pa'i pha rol na/
14b2(phal chen): jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho rin po che thams cad kyis dri ma med pa'i 'od du rnam par brgyan pa zhes bya ba yod do//de'i dbus na 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa
14b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'od dang /smon lam gyi dbyangs zhes bya ba yod do//de'i dbus na 'jig rten gyi khamos rin po che thams cad kyi sprin sna tshogs dang ldan pa/'jig rten gyi 'og gi mtshan
14b4(phal chen): nas rin po che thams cad kyi 'phreng ba'i dra ba rgya mtsho so brtan pa/rin po che'i rgyal po spos kyi rdo rje thams cad kyi rgyan gyi lhun dang ldan pa/khang pa brtsegs pa rgya'i dbyingasu 'dug pa
14b5(phal chen): rnam par dag cing kun nas nyon mongs pa/lha rdzas kyi gzhol med khang dang gnas gyi sprin gyis kun tu gang ba gser ltar dri ma med pa'i 'od kyi rgyan ces bya ba yod pa dor bskol pa kun tu
14b6(phal chen): snang ba'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba byung ste/'jig rten gyi khams de na snying po byang chub rin po che thams cad kyi snying po 'od sna tshogs can zhes bya ba yod do/der bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
14b7(phal chen): gshegs pa phyir mi ldog po'i chos kyi dbyings kyi dbyangs shes bya ba/bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas te/de'i tshe de'i dus na/kho ma yang snying po
15a1(phal chen): byang chub kyi lha mo bsod nams sgron ma phun sum tshogs pa kun nas dpal gyi 'od ces bya ba zhig du gyur te/byang chub kyi shing de la 'dug 'dug nas der kho mos
15a2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa de mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa mthong nas/bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do//de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong
15a3(phal chen): nas kyang kho mos de bzhin gshegs pa'i ston rgya mtsho'i 'od ces bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//de'i 'og tu 'jig rten gyi khams de nyid kyi rgyal po'i gnas kun nas yongasu rgyas pa'i
15a4(phal chen): dpal gyi snying po zhes bya bar snying po byang chub de nyid du/de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sdong po ri bo bzi brjid ces bya ba mngon par sangs rgyaso//kho mos ni de nas shi 'phos
15a5(phal chen): te/snying po byang chub de nyid du ye shes phun sum tshogs pa'i bsod nams 'od ces bya ba'i mtshan mo'i lha mo zhig tu gyur cing 'dug 'dug ste/kho mos der bcom ldan 'das de
15a6(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sdong po ri bo'i gzi brjid des chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa mthong nas/'gro ba thams cad du yongasu ston pa'i mnyam pa nyid kyi
15a7(phal chen): 'od kyi yul zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi rgya mtsho thams cad kyi gsung gi rgyal po zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur
15b1(phal chen): te/de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu chos thams cad kyi yang dag par 'phel bar byed pa'i gnas shes bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de nyid du de
15b2(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa rin po che'i 'od gzer sgron ma'i rgyal mtshan rgyal po zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur te/de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu/kho mos sangs rgyas rgya mtsho rab tu snang
15b3(phal chen): ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sprin skra'i rgyal po zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur te/de bzhin gshegs pa de
15b4(phal chen): mthong mo thag tu kho mos chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgro na ma zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mo lha'i bu mo zhig tu gyur te/snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa
15b5(phal chen): ye shes skar mnga' snang ba'i rgyal po zhes bya ba bskyon bkur te/de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu kho mos sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i sgron ma
15b6(phal chen): snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin 'thob//de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa chos rnam par 'phrul pa'i shugs kyi rgyal mtshan dpal zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur
15b7(phal chen): te/de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu/kho mos dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang dag par 'jug pa'i snying po'i snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//
16a1(phal chen): de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang chub de nyid du/de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sgron ma ye shes kyi rnam par gnon pa zhes bya ba bsnyen bkur te/de bzhin gshegs
16a2(phal chen): pa de mthong ma thag tu 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du ye shes thogs pa med pa'i 'khor lo snang ba'i gzi brjid ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mos snying po byang
16a3(phal chen): chub de nyid du de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes kyi stobs kyi ri bo'i gzi brjid ces bya ba bsnyen bkur te/de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag tu kho mos dus gsum gyi sems can+da
16a4(phal chen): gyi spyod pa dang /dbang po rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//rigs kyi bu da ltar kho mas 'jig rten gyi khams gser ltar dri ma med pa'i 'od der bskal nga kun tu snang ba
16a5(phal chen): rgyurgyal mtshan la de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed cig bsnyen bkur to//thal la ni lha'i dbang por gyur te bsnyen bkur to//la la ni klu'i dbang
16a6(phal chen): bor gyur te bsnyen bkur to//la la ni gnod sbyin gyi dbang por gyur pas/la la ni dri za'i dbang por gyur pas/la la ni lha ma yin gyi dbang por gyur pas/la la ni na mkha' ldang
16a7(phal chen): gi dbang por gyur pas/la la ni mi 'am ci'i dbang por gyur pas/la la ni lto 'phye chen po'i dbang por gyur pas/la laM ni ma'i dbang por gyur pas/la la ni tshangs pa'i
16b1(phal chen): dbang por gyur pas/la la ni ltar gyur pas/la la ni mir gyur pas/la la ni bud mod du gyur pas/lA la ni skyes par gyur pas/la la ni khye'ur gyur pas/la la ni bu nor
16b2(phal chen): gyur pas bsnyen bkur te/de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyang kho mos mchod pa'o yo byad ci bdog pas mchod//de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyang rim gror
16b3(phal chen): byas so//de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyi chos bstan pa yang thos so//de nas kho mo shi 'phos nas 'jig rten gyi khams de nyid du bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul
16b4(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed cig du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad do//de nas shi 'phos nas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyun gyis brgyan pa 'di'i 'jig rten
16b5(phal chen): gyi khams mi mdzad du skyes te/kho mos bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa log par dad stsol bsnyen bkur to//de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu kho mos mun pa'i rdul
16b6(phal chen): thams cad dang bral bso rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mos de bzhin gshegs pa gser thub bsnyen bkur te/de bzhin gshegs pa de mthong ma thag
16b7(phal chen): tu kho mos zhing rgya mtsho thams cad snang ba rje su 'phro bar bya bas rgyas par 'gengs pa zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin 'thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mos de bzhin gshegs pa bsod skyabs bsnyen
17a1(phal chen): bkur te/de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu/kho mos sems can thams cad kyi skad rgya mtshor 'brug sgra sgrogs pa'i sgra dbyangs shes bya ba'i tang
17a2(phal chen): 'dzin 'thob bo//de'i 'og tu kho mos bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad 'di bsnyen bkur te/de snying po byang chub la de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par
17a3(phal chen): rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i sgo rgya mtsho/sems kyi skad cig re re la yongasu ston pa mdzad pa mthong nas/kho mos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa
17a4(phal chen): dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa 'di thob bo//de thob ma thag tu chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med
17a5(phal chen): pa'i yang brjod du med pa phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la zhugs par gyur to//chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho dag thams cad du gtogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing
17a6(phal chen): ji snyed pa de dag la rdul shin tu phra ba ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba re re l-i yang /sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul
17a7(phal chen): shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing la zhugs te mthong bar gyur to//sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag thams cad las/sangs rgyas kyi zhing re ren yang /bcom ldan 'das rnam par
17b1(phal chen): snang mdzad snying po byang chub du gshegs te/sems kyi skad cig re re la mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yongasu ston par mdzad cing mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya
17b2(phal chen): ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa re res kyang chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho rgyas par 'gengs pa mdzad pa mthong //de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad las de bzhin gshegs pa re re'i zhabs
17b3(phal chen): kyi drung na yang bdag mngon du 'dug par shes par gyur to//'jig rten gyi khams de dag du de bzhin gshegs pa snying po byang chub la bzhugs pa de dag gis chos bstan pa de dag thang
17b4(phal chen): kyang thos par gyur to//de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyi ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas sprul pa rgya mtsho byung ste/chos kyi sprin rgya mtsho rab tu sgrog pa dang rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs
17b5(phal chen): yongasu ston pa mdzad cing /chos kyi dbyings kyi phyogs rgya mtsho thams cad du gtogs pa'i zhing rgya mtsho thams cad dang 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad dang /'jig rten gyi khams
17b6(phal chen): 'byam klas pa thams cad kyi sems can 'bya mo klas pa thams cad 'gro ba'i rgyud sna tshog su skyes pa dag gi nang na sems can gyi bsam pa'i dbang du 'du shes kyi rnam pa sna tshogs kyis
17b7(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba de dag thams cad kyang yongasu 'dzin to//khong du chud par byed do//nges par rtogs par byed do//don dang tshig dang yi ge 'dzin pa'i shugs kyis rnam par
18a1(phal chen): gnon pa'i gzungs kyi mthus yongasu 'dzin to//chos kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par dag pa'i snying po khong du chud pa'i shes rab kyis yongasu sbyor ngo //
18a2(phal chen): chos rgya mtsho thams cad rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa'i rigs pas khong du chud par byed//dus gsum ltar rnam par yangs pa'i blos rgyas par 'geng so//de bzhin gshegs pa
18a3(phal chen): dang mnyam pa nyid kyi rjesu 'gro ba'i shes rab kyi mnyam par byed cing chos kyi tshul thams cad mngon par sgrub po//tshul thams cad la mdo sde'i sprin mngon par smra bo//mdo sde'i
18a4(phal chen): sprin thams cad las ches rgya mtsho yongasu gzhog pa byed do//chos rgya mtsho thams cad la chos kyi rgyud thams cad yang dag par gzhol bar byed do//chos kyi rgyud thams cad la
18a5(phal chen): chos kyi sprin yongasu shes par byed do//chos kyi sprin thams cad la chos kyi rlabs yongasu skyedado//chos kyi rlabs thams cad la chos kyi dka' ba'i shugs rgya mtsho rab tu thob par
18a6(phal chen): byed do//chos kyi dga' ba'i shugs rgya mtsho thams cad las rab tu thob par bya ba'i shugs mngon par sgrub po//sa'i shugs thams cad la ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho'i shugs mngon
18a7(phal chen): por sgrub bo//ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho'i sprin thams cad la sangs rgyas mthong ba rgya mtsho rab tu thob par byed do//sangs rgyas mthong ba rgya mtsho thams cad la snang ba rgya mtsho rab tu thob
18b1(phal chen): par byed do//snang ba rgya mtsho thams cad la dus gsum gyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gyis yongasu gzhog pa byed do//phyogs rgya mtsho mtha' dang dpung med pa rgyas par dgang ba'i tshul dang
18b2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi mtha'i spyod pa rgya mtsho tshad med pa la 'jug pa'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi sbyor ba rgya mtsho tshad med pa'i ye shes snang ba'i tshul dang /de
18b3(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i dka' ba tshad med po yongasu btang ba'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims kyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yongasu
18b4(phal chen): dag pa snang bar bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i bzod pa'i sa tshad med pa yongs spang ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i brtson 'grus chen po'i shugs tshad med pa rnam
18b5(phal chen): par 'phel bar bya ba'i mthu'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsam gtan gyi dkyil 'khor dang /bsam gtan gyi yan lag rgya mtsho tshad med
18b6(phal chen): pa yong su dag par bya ba'i sbyor bas snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul rgya mtsho tshad med pa yongasu dag par bya ba dang /rna
18b7(phal chen): par dmigs pa snang bar bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul rgya mtsho tshad med pa la 'jug par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs
19a1(phal chen): /pa'i smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul rgyu mtsha tshad med pa la 'jug par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams dang /ye shes rgyu
19a2(phal chen): stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa tshad med pa la gnas par bya ba dang /yongasu 'phel bar bya ba'i ye shes rab tu thob par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi pha
19a3(phal chen): rol tu phyin pa'i tshul rgya mtsho tshad med pa la rnam par spyad pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ba'i yongasu sgrub pa'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i sa
19a4(phal chen): yongasu gnan pa mdzad pa'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob por bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa yongasu gnon pa'i mtshams kyi rnam par 'phrul pa tshad med pas bskal
19a5(phal chen): pa rgya mtshor gnas par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i sa'i dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yongasu gnon pa'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs
19a6(phal chen): pa'i sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i' sa tshad med pa la gnas par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa'i sa tshad med pa yong su dag par bya ba'i
19a7(phal chen): tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa tshad med pa ye shes rgya mtshos rnam par dpyad pa'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshogs pa'i sa'i ye shes snang ba tshad med par rab tu thob par
19b1(phal chen): bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpar gyur pas sngon gyi sangs rgyas ma lus par gzigs pa dang /rjesu 'drang ba mdzad pa tshad med pa rnam par dmigs par
19b2(phal chen): bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpar gyur pas/sngon gyi sangs rgyas rgya mtsho ma lus par gzigs shing bskal pa rgya mtshor bzhugs bzhugs pa tshad med
19b3(phal chen): pa'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa sngon byang chub sems dpar gyur pas zhing rgya mtsho ma lus pa rgyas par dgang ba'i sku mngon par bsgrub pa tshad med pa'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob
19b4(phal chen): par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa tshad med pas chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa rgyas par dgang po'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sngon gyi
19b5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thabs sna tshogs kyi sgo dang ldan pas/sems can thams cad yongasu smin par mdzad pa dang /rnam par gdul bar mdzad pa tshad med pa yongasu bstan pa'i
19b6(phal chen): tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'odi phyogs rgya mtsho ma lus pa thams cad du rab tu 'phro ba tshad med pas rgyas par dgang bar bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa sems can thams
19b7(phal chen): cad la mngon du gyur pa rnam par 'phrul po tshad med pa yongasu bstan pa'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi sa tshad med pa yongasu gnon pa'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob par
20a1(phal chen): bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa tshad med pa'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i tshul dang /de
20a2(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu 'khor ba dang /chos kyi sprin chad med pa thams cad ma lus par yang dag par blang zhing yongasu bzung ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs
20a3(phal chen): pa'i mtshan rgya mtsho tshad med pa rnam par dmigs pa'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rgya mtsho'i rgyud tshad med pa rnam par dmigs pa snang bar
20a4(phal chen): tu thob par bya ba'i tshul dang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul shin tu yangs pa'i ye shes snang ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i tshul gyis de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi thog mthugs bskyed
20a5(phal chen): pa nas/dam pa'i chos nub par ma gyur pa'i bar de dag thams cad la'ang 'jug cing khong du chud par byed//de skad du khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thur pa dga' ba
20a6(phal chen): yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas/sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa 'di thob nas/ji srid cig len zhes zer ba ni/de ltar khams bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gnyis kyi
20a7(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol gyi 'jig rten gyi khams gser ltar dri ma med pa'i 'od tu byang chub kyi shing gi lha mo bsod nams skyon ma phun sum tshogs pa kun nas dpal
20b1(phal chen): gyi 'od ces bya bar gyur te/de bzhin gshegs pa phyir mi ldog pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyi dbyangs kyi chos bstan pa thos nas/bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed//
20b2(phal chen): bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing gnyis kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed po de dag tu byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad nas/mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir skyes te/log par dad sol
20b3(phal chen): la sogs pa tha ma shAkya thub pa'i bar gyi de bzhin gshegs pa bskal pa bzang po dag kyang bsnyen bkur te//ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyang bsnyen bkur to//'jig rten gyi khams
20b4(phal chen): 'dir ji lta ba de bzhin du/'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du'ang /sangs rgyas kyi rgyud ma byon pa rnams yongasu bsnyen cing bkuro//mchod de//rigs kyi bu da dung du'ang 'jig rten
20b5(phal chen): gyi khams gser ltar dri ma med pa'i 'od de yang yod la/sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyang rkyen ma tshad kyis/de bas ni rigs kyi bu tshul 'di la byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par gnon po chen
20b6(phal chen): ngos brjon par gyis shig/de nas mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pas/de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba sangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas/sems
20b7(phal chen): kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa 'di nyid brtan te bstan par bya ba'i phyir/tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la tshog su bcang de smras pa/rnam thar dge 'di ji ltar thob gyur pa//kho mo'i tshing
21a1(phal chen): 'di nor bzangs khyod nyon cig/thos nas dga' ba'i stobs kyang yongs skyed de//rnam thar tshul 'di la ni 'jug par gyis//bdag gi sems dang bsam pa
21a2(phal chen): yongs sbyong zhing //mos pa'i shugs yangs yongasu bskyed byas te//thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes grong 'dun pas//bskal pa rgya mtsho mang por sngon spyad do//bde gsheg
21a3(phal chen): dus gsum byung ba thos nas kyang //de dag kun la mos po yongs skyed do//bskal pa brgya phrag mang por sgo kun tu//de dag 'khor dang bcas par kho mos bkur//sngon gyi bdi
21a4(phal chen): gshegs kho mos mthong gyur na//'gro la phan phyir yun ring mchod byas te//spro ba'i stobs ni rnam yangs yongs bskyed nas//bdag gis gdung ba med pa'i chos kyang thos//
21a5(phal chen): rnam par thar pa 'di la 'jug pa na//pha dang ma dang bla ma'i skye bo la//de tshe bdag gis phan bdes sti stang byas//bsnyon bkur sri zhur gnas pa kun kyang byas//rgas pa nad pa nor
21a6(phal chen): med mi rnams dang //dbang po ma tshang sdug bsngal mgon mod pa//mang po bdag gis byams sems bde bkod nas//tshe rab brgyar yang nor phyag mgon yod byas//rgyal po
21a7(phal chen): me dang rkun chos rkyen gyur dang //seng ge glang po pha rol dgra 'jigs dang //srid pa'i rgya mtsho'i 'jigs dngos sna tshogs las//sngon tshe spyod pa'i dus na bdag gis bskyabs///
21b1(phal chen): rtag tu srid gsum nyon mongs gdungs gyur te//las kyis rab gdungs de bzhin mi dge bas//'khor ba'i ri gzar g.yang du lhung ba yi//skye bo 'gro ba'i rgyud du bdag gis bskyabs//
21b2(phal chen): sdug bsngal ngan song g.yang sas 'jigs pa dag/rtag tu mi bde shin tu mi bzad dang //skye rgan zhing 'chi ba'i 'jigs mang kun//bdag gis 'dzeg rten spyod che zhi bar byas//
21b3(phal chen): 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal zhi bar bya ba dang //sems can kun gyi bde ba yongs bskyed cing //sangs rgyas bde ba dam pa bskyed pa ni//bskal pa phyi mar kho mo'i smon lam mo//ring/
21b4(phal chen): kyi bu kho mos byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas/sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa 'di shes par zad na/kho mos byang chub sems
21b5(phal chen): dpa' chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la zhugs pa/phyi nang gi sdug bsngal ma lus pa las rnam par grol ba/bskal pa'i ming du bya ba thams cad shes par gyur pa/'jig
21b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad 'byung ba dang /'jig pa'i rgyus la mkhas pa de dag gi spyod pa shes pa 'am/ston brjod par nus re skan/song rigs kyi bu snying po byang chub
21b7(phal chen): 'di na nyid na bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na/mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal zhes bya ba 'dug
22a1(phal chen): gis/de'i gan du song la/ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la bslab par bya ba dang /ji ltar nan tan du bya ba dris shig/de
22a2(phal chen): nus tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis/mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshig suM bcad pa 'di dag smras so//dge ba'i bya shes
22a3(phal chen): kyis ma nor 'dun bsten pas//lha mo khyod kyi drung du nye bar mtshos//mtha' dang dpung mi mnga' ba'i sku tshul du//khyod ni gdon la bzhugs pa bdag gis mthong //kha dog gyis
22a4(phal chen): dang mtshan mo'i spyod yul ba//srid la gnas dang dngos por 'du shes dang //'du shes dma' dang log par lta ba yis//khyod kyi spyod yul 'tshal bar mi nus so//khyod kyi sku
22a5(phal chen): gzugs blta na mtha' yas pas//khyod kyi sku gzugs mdog go mtshan ma ni//bskal pa mtha' yas dag tu yongs brtags kyang //lha dang 'jig rten bcas pas shes mi
22a6(phal chen): nus//lha mi khyod ni phung po'i gnas los 'phags//skye mched rnams la'ang de bzhin ri 'jig rten rnam par 'das pas tho tsam bral//'jig rten dag du rnam par 'phrul ba mdzad//
22a7(phal chen): go ma ba mi mapa'i sbyin bral chags pa med//khyod kyis yo shes spyan ni rnam sbyangs pa//rdul gyi gol thams cad rdul tshad du//sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul po mang ba gzigs//rgyud/
22b1(phal chen): kyisku ni chos sku'i snying po can//khyod kyi thugs kyang ye shes chags pa med//khyod ni kun tu 'od kyis snang mdzad pas//'jig rten skye bo rnams la mtha' yas snang //sems las mtha'
22b2(phal chen): yas las rnams yosu 'byung //'jig rten thams cad las kyis rnam par bris//'gro ba sems kyi dngosu mkhyen gyur pas//rang gi sku yang 'gro ba snyed du bstan//'jig rten du ni
22b3(phal chen): rmi lam 'drar mkhyen nas//sangs rgyas kun kyang gzugs brnyan lta bu dang //ma lus chos rnams sgra brnyan 'drar mkhyen pas//chags pa mi mnga' 'gro ba kun tu spyod//dus gsum
22b4(phal chen): gnas pa'i 'gro ba thams cad la//skad cig re rer rang gi sku ston kyang //khyod kyi thugs la gnyi su mi rgyu ste//phyogs rnams kun tu chos kyang rab tu bstan//rdul lo 'gro ba rgya mtsho
22b5(phal chen): mtha' yas dang //de bzhin sems can mtsho chen dpag yos drang //mtho'i dpung med pa'i bde gshegs gang chen mtsho//kun kyang khyod kyi rnam par dam pa'i yul//de nas tshong dpon
22b6(phal chen): gyi bu nor bzangs kyis//mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa la tshul dang 'dra ba'i tshigasu bcad pa de dag gis mngon par bstod de/lan brgya stong du mar g.yas
22b7(phal chen): phyogasu bskor ba byas nas yang dang yang bltas te/mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i drung nas song ngo //shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo//sangs rgyas
23a1(phal chen): phal po che zhes bya ba las/sdong pos brgyan pa'i le'u ste/bam po brgya gnyis pa//de nas tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs/byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par
23a2(phal chen): thar pa dga' ba yangs pa'i shugs 'byung bas/sems kyi skad cig rnam par brgyan pa de ni bsgom pa dang /rjesu bsgom pa dang /yang dag par bsgom pa byed/mtshan mo'i lha mo sgra
23a3(phal chen): rgya mtsho rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa'i gdams ngag rjesu bstan pa la ni rjesu 'brang bar bya ba dang /rjesu dran par bya ba dang /khong du chud par byed/tshig dang yi ge re re la ni tshul du ma dang
23a4(phal chen): bsam pa tshad med pas chos nyid kyi tshul shes pa rjesu dran par byed cing /dran pas rjesu 'brang bar bya ba dang /blo gros kyis rnam par bya ba dang /rigs pas khong du chud par bya ba dang /blos
23a5(phal chen): shin tu yangs par bya ba dang /lus kyis reg par bya ste/rnam par spyad pa dang /rje su 'jug pa byed cing /mthar gyis mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i
23a6(phal chen): gzi brjid dpal gang na ba der phyin pa dang /mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyekhyor thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal pad+mo'i khri chen po nor du rin po che'i rgyal po grong khyer dang /gnas
23a7(phal chen): thams cad rab tu snang bar byed pa'i snying po can la phyogs thams cad dang /'gro ba thams cad la mngon du gyur pa lus dang /'gro ba thams cad kyi gzugs dang mnyam pa'i lus dang //
23b1(phal chen): sems can thams cad la mngon du gyur pa'i lus dang /'gro ba thams cad kyis mgos pa'i lus dang /'gro ba thams cad dang rang bzhin mnyam pa'i lus dang /'gro ba thams cad las
23b2(phal chen): mngon par 'phags pa'i lus dang /'gro ba thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang /gdul ba la 'thun pa'i lus dang /'gro ba thams cad du sgra rab tu sgrog pa'i lus dang /'gro ba thad
23b3(phal chen): du 'pho ba med pa'i lus dang /sgrib pa thams cad shin tu bcom pa'i lus dang /de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin gyi lus dang /'gro ba thams cad gdul ba mthar phyin par byed pa'i lus su
23b4(phal chen): 'dug cing mtshan mo'i lha mo brjod du med pa'i 'khor gyi bskor te/'dug pa mthong nas dga' rangs te mgu zhing nyams bde la tshim zhing yid bde ba skyes nas/mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer
23b5(phal chen): thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i rkang pa gnyis la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal la/lan brgya stong du mar g.yos
23b6(phal chen): phyogasu bskor ba byas nas/mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyi mdun du 'dug te/thal mo sbyar nas 'di skad ces smraso//lha mo bdag bla
23b7(phal chen): noni med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs na/lha mo ji ltar byang chub sems dpas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod po la rjesu bslabs na/sems can la sman par
24a1(phal chen): 'gyur ba lags/ji ltar na sems can bla na med pa yosu bsgrubs yongasu sdud par 'gyur/ji myur na byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pas gnang
24a2(phal chen): pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i las la brtson pa lags/ji ltar brtson par bgyis na/byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi rgyal por nye bar 'gyur ba bdag la bshad du gsol/de skad ces
24a3(phal chen): smras pa dang /mtshan mo'i lha mo grong khyer thams cad bsrung ba 'byung ba'i gzi brjid dpal gyis/tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la 'di skad ces smraso//rigs kyi bu khyod de ltar 'gro
24a4(phal chen): ba thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang /rnam par gdul ba'i mthar phyin par bya ba dang /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs yang dag par bzung ba'i sbyor ba mthar phyin par bya
24a5(phal chen): ba dang /phyogs 'byam klas pa thams cad rgyas par dgang ba'i ye shes rab tu sbyor ba dang /chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul rgya mtsho thams cad la 'jug pa mngon du 'gyur ba dang /shes bya
24a6(phal chen): namakha'i dbyings dang /mnyam par mtha' yas pa rgyas par dgang ba dang /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu blang zhing yongasu bzung ba'i phyir/'gro ba rgya
24a7(phal chen): mtsho thamaso cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par dbab pa'i spyod pa'i tshul yongasu 'dri ba legaso legs so//rigs kyi bu kho mo ni byang chub sems
24b1(phal chen): dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ang ba dang /rnam par 'khrul pa za' mo la 'jug pa thob pa ste/de ltar kho mo rnam par thar pa de dang ldan pas/chos smra ba chen po'i go 'phang thogs pa med
24b2(phal chen): pa la dmigs pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/de bzhin gshegs pa tha~Md kyi chos kyi mdzod yongasu btang ba'i smon lam dang ldan pa/snying rje chen po dang ldan pa byams pa chen po'i stobs rab tu thob
24b3(phal chen): pa sems can thams cad byang chub kyi sems la dgod pa'i phyir/sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba la zhugs pa/byang chub kyi sems kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba dang /tshogs rab tu bsags pa
24b4(phal chen): rgyun mi gcad pa'i phyir 'gro ba thams cad kha lo sgyur ba'i so la yang dag par gnas pa/sems can thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi lam la rab tu dgod pa'i phyir/'jig rten
24b5(phal chen): gyi chos gyi sprin thams cad las chos kyi nyi ma yongasu dbyung ba'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa bskyed pas 'jig rten thams cad snang bar bya ba'i phyir/'gro ba thams cad mnye
24b6(phal chen): pa'i semasu 'jug pa'i rgyun mi 'chad pa/'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon par 'du bya ba yongasu bsgrub pa'i sbyor ba shes par bya ba'i phyir/sems rnam par dag pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan
24b7(phal chen): pa/dge ba'i las kyi lam thams cad 'thun par sgrub pas/sems can thams cad kyi ded dpon du zhugs pa/mi dge ba'i las kyi lam thams cad rab tu spangs pa/sems can thams cad dge
25a1(phal chen): ba'i chos la rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan bya/sems can thams cad la lam bde ba yongasu ston pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/sems can thams cad
25a2(phal chen): theg pa'i rgyun gyi thog mar 'dren pa la zhugs pa/dge ba'i chos kyi spyod pa thams cad la sems can thams cad rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams
25a3(phal chen): cad la mi phyed par bsnyen bkur dang /rim gro byed pa la zhugs pa/sems can thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa la rab tu dgod pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/chos kyi
25a4(phal chen): sbyin pa'i sngon 'dren cing /chos dkar po thams cad yang dag par brtsams pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed pas/mngon par byung bas bas
25a5(phal chen): po gtan zhing mi shigs pa/rdo rje mthu bo che ltar bstan zhing srabs sangs rgyas kyi stobs la dmigs pa'i sems rgya chen po'i dkyil 'khor dang ldan par dge ba'i bshes gnyen
25a6(phal chen): la rton cing rnam par spyod do//kho mon nyon mongs pa dang /las kyi sgrib pa thams cad kyi ri rnam par gtor ba'i sems dang ldan pa'o//thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi tshogs yang dag
25a7(phal chen): par rtsom pa'o//dkor po'i chos thams cad yang dag par bsgrub pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa'o//thams cad mkhyen pa nyid mtha' dang dpung med pa la mngon par 'dun cing dmigs
25b1(phal chen): pa'i sems kyi sbyor ba la brtson pa'o//rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mo chos snang ba'i sgo sems can thams cad yongasu rton pa rnam pa de lta bu yongs sbyong zhing dge ba'i rtsa ba bstsags pa'i tshogs la
25b2(phal chen): sta bon du gnas pas/rnam pa bcus chos kyi dbyings la rnam par lta zhing khong du chud pa dang /rjesu gzhol bar byed do//bcu gang zhe na/'od lta ste/ye shes snang ba shin tu bcangs pa
25b3(phal chen): thob pas chos kyi dbyings ni tshad med par khong du chud par byed do//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni mtha' dang dpung
25b4(phal chen): med par khong du chud par byed do//sangs rgyas kyi zhing tha~Md yongasu gnan pa dang /de bzhin gshegs pa mchod cing rim gror bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni mu med par khong du chud par byed//
25b5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du/byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongasu bstan pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni sa mtshams med par khong du chud par byed do//de bzhin gshog
25b6(phal chen): pa'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor tha mi dad pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni ris chad pa med par khong du chud par byed do//bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sems can thams cad kyis
25b7(phal chen): rnam par dmigs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung gi dkyil 'khor la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur par khong du chud par byed do//'gro ba
26a1(phal chen): /thams cad rnam par gla lta ba'i mang rgyungs/da nan gshegs bya stan tu las kyi mtha drug+sa pa ldum pa ba b+h+yo/ts+tshos nA~M
26a2(phal chen): ni rang bshin gyis rgya che bar khong du chud par byed do//byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'ibyam kris pa la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir/chos kyi dbyings ni 'gro ba thams cad
26a3(phal chen): la mnyam pa nyid du gyur par khong du chud par byed do//kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan lo 'jug par bya ba'i phyir/chosna kyi dbyings ni rgyun cig tu gyur par
26a4(phal chen): khong du chud par byed do//dge ba thams cad kyis chos kyi dbyings rgyas por dgang zhing rnam par dag par bya ba chud mi za bo'i chos can du bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings ni thub pa
26a5(phal chen): med par khong du chud par byed do//rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mo rnam pa bcu po de dag gis dge ba'i rtsa ba dang /tshogs thams cad yongasu bsagaso pa dang /sangs rgyas kyu bdag
26a6(phal chen): nyid che ba nyid la 'jug par bya ba dang /sangs rgyas kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa rdza su rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/chos kyi dbyings thams cad la rnam par blta ba'o//khong
26a7(phal chen): chud pa dang rdza su gzhol bar byed do//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang kho mo de ltar de bzhin gshegs po'i bdog nyid che ba nyid kyi rje su 'brang ba'i yid la bya ba dang ldan pas/gzung
26b1(phal chen): kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyud stong phrag bcus sems can rnams la chos ston te/bcu gang zhe na/'di ltar chos rgya mtsho thams cad yang dag par 'du ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil
26b2(phal chen): 'khor dang /chos thams cad byin gyis rlob pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /chos kyi sprin thams cad yongasu 'dzin pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /de bzhin gshegs pa
26b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi dgongs pa sgron ma'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtsho rab tu snang bar byed pa'i snying po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /theg pa'i
26b4(phal chen): tshul rgya mtsho dri ma med pa thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad kyi sgron ma'i snying po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /
26b5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan gyi 'khor lo'i glong rab tu sgrog pa'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi sngon gyi smon lam rgya mtsho bstan
26b6(phal chen): pa la yang dag par gzhol ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /chos thams cad la mngon par 'khyil ba'i shugs drag po'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /thams cad mkhyen
26b7(phal chen): pa nyid kyi shugs rab tu 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor dang /rigs kyi bu gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor bcu po de dag la sogs pa gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyud
27a1(phal chen): stong phrag bcus sems can namasA la chos ston te//rigs kyi bu gzhan yang khoms ni thos pa'i shes rab kyis sems can rnams la chos ston te/
27a2(phal chen): bsams pa'i shes rab dang /bsgoms pa'i shes rab kyis sems can rnams la chos ston te/srid pa'i rgyud cig las kyang bsnams shing sems can rnams la chos
27a3(phal chen): ston to//srid pa'i rgyud rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang bsnams shing sems can rnams la chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi mtshan gyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las
27a4(phal chen): kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan gyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//'jig rten gyi khams rgya
27a5(phal chen): mtsho gcig las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang /bsnams shing chos ston to//sangs rgyas gcig gi lung bston
27a6(phal chen): pa las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi lung bstan pa rgya mtsho las kyang bsdums shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi
27a7(phal chen): 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho las kyang bskyams shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho las kyang bsnams shing chos ston
27b1(phal chen): to//de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi 'khor lo las kyang bskums shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo rgya mtsho las kyang bsnams
27b2(phal chen): shing chos ston to//mdo sde gcig pa las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo la yang dag par gzhol ba'i mdo sde las kyang
27b3(phal chen): bsnams shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor kun nas 'dus pa las kyang bskyams shing chos ston to//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
27b4(phal chen): kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor kun nas 'dus pa rgya mtsho las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems gcig las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//byang
27b5(phal chen): chub kyi sems kyi yan lag rgya mtsho thams cad las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//theg pa gcig las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//theg pa thams cad kyis 'byung ba rgya
27b6(phal chen): mtsho las kyang bsnams shing chos ston to//rigs kyi bu de ltar kho mo bstan pa'i tshul mngon par bsgrub pa brjod du med pas sems can rnams la chos ston to//rigs kyi bu de ltar
27b7(phal chen): kho mo chos kyi dbyings kyi tshul tha mi dad pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rgya mtsho la 'jug cing sems can thams cad la chos ston pas/bla na med pa'i yongasu bsdu ba byed cing /byang chub
28a1(phal chen): sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa rgya mtshor gnas par bya bas/byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong
28a2(phal chen): ba dang /rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa 'di la sems kyi skad cig re re zhing rnam par 'phel ba'i rnam par thar pa'i yul bsgom pa'i tshul gyis yongasu bsgom ste/rnam par thar
28a3(phal chen): pa'i yul bsgom pa'i tshul re res kyang /sems kyi skad cig re re la chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rgyas par 'gengaso//nor bzangs kyis smras pa/lha mo byang chub sems dpa'i rnam pa
28a4(phal chen): thar pa de de ltar bzab pa ngo mtshar che na/'phags ma khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa 'di brnyes nas ji srid cig lags/skyes pa rigs kyi bu sngon 'das pa'i dus bskal
28a5(phal chen): pa 'jig rten gyi rgyud kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol cig tu 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi 'od 'phro ba'i grong khyer dpal gyi sprin ces bya ba rin po che spros thams cad dang ldan pa/
28a6(phal chen): gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi spo la blangs pa/de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi smon lam dbyangasu sgrog pa'i pad+mos mtshams rnam par brgyan
28a7(phal chen): pa/lhun sems can thams cad kyi las rgya mtshos byung ba'i nor bu rin pa che'i rgyal po rgya mtsho las grub pa pad+mo chen po'i dbyingasu 'dug pa rnam par dag cing /kun nas nyon mongs pa me tog
28b1(phal chen): gokhar yug ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis kun nus bskor ba/spros kyi rin pa che ri rab kyi rum shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rgyan ring ba lhur mngon par 'phags pa dang ldan pa gleng ban pa chen du
28b2(phal chen): re rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/gling pon pa re re zhing yang grod rdal bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dang ldan pa byung ngo //rigs kyibu
28b3(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams de'i bskal pa mdog dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba byung ste/bskum pa de la de bzhin gshegs pa ri rab kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byung ngo //'jig rten gyi khams
28b4(phal chen): chos kyi 'od 'gro ba'i grong khyer dpal gyi sprin gyi gling bzhi pa dbu ma rgyal mtshan sna tshogs shes bya ba byung ste/de'i dbus na rgyal po'i gnas rin chen mo tog kun tu snang ba zhes bya ba yod par gyur
28b5(phal chen): tAM/rgyal po'i gnas de dang ha cang yang mo ring ba zhig na/snying po byang chub chos kyi rgyal po'i po dri rdzob tu snang ba zhes bya ba yod de/snying po byang chub de la de bzhin gau shegs pa ri ra
28b6(phal chen): kyi rdul shin tu phra bsnyed po de dag gi bskal pa'i dang po la/de bzhin gshegs pa chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyangs/'od kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba byung ste/de'i tshe 'khor los sgyur
28b7(phal chen): nga'i rgyal po nyi mi ltar bzhin mdag dri ma med pa zhes bya ba byung nas/des bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs po chos rgya mtshathams cad kyi dbyings nyid kyi rgyal po las mang snga tshas
29a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi glong rgya mtsho zhes bya ba yongasu bzung ste/bzung nas kyang chos kyi 'khor lo rjesu bskor to//yongasu mya ngan las 'das nas kyang rab tu byung ste/bstan
29a2(phal chen): pa yongasu bzung ngo //bstan pa nub du cha ste/bstan pa yang stong du gyis/chos bstan pa shin tu bstan pa'i tshul ni brgya phrag bcur gyur/rnyog pa'i bskal pa bar ma ni nye bar gan
29a3(phal chen): par gyur pa'i tshe/sems can las dang nyon mongs pa'i sgribs pas sgribs pa thab mo dang spyod pa dang dkrugs ma la zhugs par gyur pa dang /dge slong sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i ston
29a4(phal chen): don du mi gnyer cing yul gyi dga' ba lhur len par gyur pa/rgyal po dang rkun po'i gtam la zhugs pa/bud med dang yul dang rgya mtsho'i gtam la mos pa/'jig rten rgyang ban
29a5(phal chen): pa'i tshig la zhugs pa rnams yongasu skye ba bskyed pa'i phyir/kye ma'o bskal pa du mar yongasu bsgrubs pa'i chos kyi sgron ma chen po ni nub par gyur ma khad do zhes chos dang ldan pa'i'o
29a6(phal chen): dod bos te/yongasu skyo bar 'gyur ba'i gtam byas nas/de steng gi na mkha' dbyings ta la bdun tsam du mngon par 'phags nas/'od 'phro ba kha dog mtha' yas pa'i sprin rab tu
29a7(phal chen): bkye ste/'od gzer gyi dra ba'i rgyan chen po kha dog sna tshogs dang ldan pa bkye nas/'od kha dog du ma dang ldan pas/'jig rten gyi nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba zhi bar byas ste/sems
29b1(phal chen): can mtha' dang dpung med pa dag kyang byang chub la rab tu bkod do//de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa de yang phyir gsal bar byas te/lo stong phrag drug bcur gnas par gyur to//
29b2(phal chen): de'i tshe 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po nyi ma ltar bzhin mdog dri ma med pa de nyid kyi bu mo dge slong ma chos kyi 'khor los sprul po'i 'od ces bya ba dge slong ma brgya phrag stong gi 'khor dang
29b3(phal chen): ldan pa byung ste//des yongasu skyo bar 'gyur ba'i sgra de thos nas/cho 'phrul chen po de mthang ste/'khor dang bcas pas byang chub tu sems bskyed nas/dge slong ma brgyu phrag stong
29b4(phal chen): bib de dag kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog pa byas te/de bzhin gshegs pa mngon du 'gyur ba la yang dag par gzhol ba zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin
29b5(phal chen): kyang rab tu thob par gyur to//de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor los sprul pa'i 'od ces bya ba'i gzungs kyang rab tu thob bo//chos rgya mtsho'i tshul thams cad la 'jug
29b6(phal chen): pa zhes bya ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang rab tu thob par gyur to//dge slong ma chos kyi 'khor los sprul pa'i 'od kyis kyang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bstan pa las byung
29b7(phal chen): ba'i 'od kyi sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang /byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa sgra yid du 'ong ba dang rnam par 'phrul pa zab mo la 'jug pa 'di yang shin tu phra zhing 'jam pa'i
